1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-957">在“输入要选择的对象名称”区域中输入 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-957">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-958">选择“检查名称”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-958">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-959">有关 DefaultAppPool，请检查使用 IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool 的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-959">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-960">当选择“检查名称”按钮时，对象名称区域中会显示 DefaultAppPool 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-960">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-961">无法直接在对象名称区域中输入应用池名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-961">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-962">检查对象名称时，请使用 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** 格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-962">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![应用文件夹的“选择用户或组”对话框：在选择“检查名称”前，将“DefaultAppPool\"”的应用池名称追加到对象名称区域中的“IIS AppPool”。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-964">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-964">Select **OK** .</span></span>

   ![应用文件夹的“选择用户或组”对话框：在你选择“检查名称”后，对象名称“DefaultAppPool”显示在对象名称区域中。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-966">默认情况下应授予读取 &amp; 执行权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-966">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-967">根据需要请提供其他权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-967">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-968">也可使用 ICACLS 工具在命令提示符处授予访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-968">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-969">以 DefaultAppPool 为例，使用以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-969">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-970">有关详细信息，请参阅 [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) 主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-970">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-971">HTTP/2 支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-971">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-972">以下 IIS 部署方案中的 ASP.NET Core 支持 [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-972">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported with ASP.NET Core in the following IIS deployment scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-973">进程内</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-973">In-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-974">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 或更高版本；IIS 10 或更高版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-974">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-975">TLS 1.2 或更高版本的连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-975">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-976">进程外</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-976">Out-of-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-977">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 或更高版本；IIS 10 或更高版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-977">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-978">面向公众的边缘服务器连接使用 HTTP/2，但与 [Kestrel 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)的反向代理连接使用 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-978">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-979">TLS 1.2 或更高版本的连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-979">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-980">对于已建立 HTTP/2 连接时的进程内部署，[HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) 会报告 `HTTP/2`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-980">For an in-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/2`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-981">对于已建立 HTTP/2 连接时的进程外部署，[HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) 会报告 `HTTP/1.1`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-981">For an out-of-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-982">若要详细了解进程内和进程外托管模型，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-982">For more information on the in-process and out-of-process hosting models, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-983">默认情况下将启用 HTTP/2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-983">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-984">如果未建立 HTTP/2 连接，连接会回退到 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-984">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-985">有关使用 IIS 部署的 HTTP/2 配置的详细信息，请参阅 [IIS 上的 HTTP/2](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-985">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-986">CORS 预检请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-986">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-987">本部分仅适用于面向 .NET Framework 的 ASP.NET Core 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-987">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-988">对于面向 .NET Framework 的 ASP.NET Core 应用程序，默认情况下，IIS 不会将 OPTIONS 请求传递给应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-988">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-989">若要了解如何在 web.config 中配置应用程序的 IIS 处理程序以传递 OPTIONS 请求，请参阅[在 ASP.NET Web API 2 中启用跨域请求：CORS 的工作原理](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-989">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>

## <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-990">应用程序初始化模块和空闲超时</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-990">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-991">通过 ASP.NET Core 模板版本 2 托管在 IIS 中时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-991">When hosted in IIS by the ASP.NET Core Module version 2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-992">[应用程序初始化模块](#application-initialization-module)：可以将托管在[进程内](#in-process-hosting-model)或[进程外](#out-of-process-hosting-model)的应用配置为在工作进程重启或服务器重启后自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-992">[Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) or [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) can be configured to start automatically on a worker process restart or server restart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-993">[空闲超时](#idle-timeout)：可以将托管在[进程内](#in-process-hosting-model)的应用配置为在非活动时段不超时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-993">[Idle Timeout](#idle-timeout): App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) can be configured not to timeout during periods of inactivity.</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-994">应用程序初始化模块</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-994">Application Initialization Module</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-995">适用于托管在进程内和进程外的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-995">*Applies to apps hosted in-process and out-of-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-996">[IIS 应用程序初始化](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization)是一种 IIS 功能，可在应用池启动或回收时向应用发送 HTTP 请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-996">[IIS Application Initialization](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) is an IIS feature that sends an HTTP request to the app when the app pool starts or is recycled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-997">该请求会触发应用启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-997">The request triggers the app to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-998">默认情况下，IIS 向应用的根 URL (`/`) 发出请求以初始化应用（有关配置的详细信息，请参阅[更多资源](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources)）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-998">By default, IIS issues a request to the app's root URL (`/`) to initialize the app (see the [additional resources](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources) for more details on configuration).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-999">确认已启用 IIS 应用程序初始化角色功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-999">Confirm that the IIS Application Initialization role feature in enabled:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1000">Windows 7 或更高版本桌面系统，在本地使用 IIS 时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1000">On Windows 7 or later desktop systems when using IIS locally:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1001">导航到“控制面板”>“程序”>“程序和功能”>“打开或关闭 Windows 功能”（位于屏幕左侧）   。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1001">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1002">打开“Internet Information Services”>“万维网服务”>“应用程序开发功能”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1002">Open **Internet Information Services** > **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1003">选中“应用程序初始化”的复选框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1003">Select the check box for **Application Initialization** .</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1004">Windows Server 2008 R2 或更高版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1004">On Windows Server 2008 R2 or later:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1005">打开“添加角色和功能向导”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1005">Open the **Add Roles and Features Wizard** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1006">在“选择角色服务”面板中，打开“应用程序开发”节点 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1006">In the **Select role services** panel, open the **Application Development** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1007">选中“应用程序初始化”的复选框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1007">Select the check box for **Application Initialization** .</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1008">使用下面的任一方法为站点启用“应用程序初始化模块”：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1008">Use either of the following approaches to enable the Application Initialization Module for the site:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1009">使用 IIS 管理器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1009">Using IIS Manager:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1010">在“连接”面板中选择“应用程序池”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1010">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1011">在列表中右键单击应用的应用池，并选择“高级设置”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1011">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings** .</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1012">默认的“启动模式”为“按需” 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1012">The default **Start Mode** is **OnDemand** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1013">将“启动模式”设置为“始终运行”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1013">Set the **Start Mode** to **AlwaysRunning** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1014">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1014">Select **OK** .</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1015">打开“连接”面板中的“网站”节点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1015">Open the **Sites** node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1016">右键单击应用，并选择“管理网站”>“高级设置” 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1016">Right-click the app and select **Manage Website** > **Advanced Settings** .</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1017">默认的“预加载已启用”设置为“False” 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1017">The default **Preload Enabled** setting is **False** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1018">将“预加载已启用”设置为“True”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1018">Set **Preload Enabled** to **True** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1019">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1019">Select **OK** .</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1020">使用 web.config 将 `doAppInitAfterRestart` 已设置为 `true` 的 `<applicationInitialization>` 元素添加到应用的 web.config 文件中的 `<system.webServer>` 元素中 ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1020">Using *web.config* , add the `<applicationInitialization>` element with `doAppInitAfterRestart` set to `true` to the `<system.webServer>` elements in the app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
  <configuration>
    <location path="." inheritInChildApplications="false">
      <system.webServer>
        <applicationInitialization doAppInitAfterRestart="true" />
      </system.webServer>
    </location>
  </configuration>
  ```

### <a name="idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1021">空闲超时</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1021">Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1022">仅适用于托管在进程内的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1022">*Only applies to apps hosted in-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1023">若要防止应用进入空闲状态，请使用 IIS 管理器设置应用池的空闲超时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1023">To prevent the app from idling, set the app pool's idle timeout using IIS Manager:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1024">在“连接”面板中选择“应用程序池”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1024">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1025">在列表中右键单击应用的应用池，并选择“高级设置”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1025">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1026">默认的“空闲超时(分钟)”为“20”分钟 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1026">The default **Idle Time-out (minutes)** is **20** minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1027">将“空闲超时(分钟)”设置为“0”（零） 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1027">Set the **Idle Time-out (minutes)** to **0** (zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1028">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1028">Select **OK** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1029">回收工作进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1029">Recycle the worker process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1030">若要防止托管在[进程外](#out-of-process-hosting-model)的应用超时，请使用下列任一方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1030">To prevent apps hosted [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) from timing out, use either of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1031">从外部服务 ping 应用，使其保持运行状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1031">Ping the app from an external service in order to keep it running.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1032">如果应用仅托管后台服务，请避免使用 IIS 托管，而是[使用 Windows 服务托管 ASP.NET Core 应用](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1032">If the app only hosts background services, avoid IIS hosting and use a [Windows Service to host the ASP.NET Core app](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1033">关于应用程序初始化模块和空闲超时的更多资源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1033">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout additional resources</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1036">[应用程序池 \<processModel> 的进程模型设置](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1036">[Process Model Settings for an Application Pool \<processModel>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel).</span></span>

## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1047">支持的操作系统</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1047">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1048">支持下列操作系统：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1048">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1049">Windows 7 或更高版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1049">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1050">Windows Server 2008 R2 或更高版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1050">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1051">[HTTP.sys 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys)（以前称为 WebListener）无法以反向代理配置形式与 IIS 结合使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1051">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1052">请使用 [Kestrel 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1052">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1053">有关在 Azure 上托管的信息，请参阅<xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1053">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1054">有关疑难解答指南，请参阅 <xref:test/troubleshoot>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1054">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1055">受支持的平台</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1055">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1056">支持针对 32 位 (x86) 或 64 位 (x64) 部署发布的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1056">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1057">使用 32 位 (x86) .NET Core SDK 部署 32 位应用，除非应用符合以下情况：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1057">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1058">需要适用于 64 位应用的更大虚拟内存地址空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1058">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1059">需要更大 IIS 堆栈大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1059">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1060">具有 64 位本机依赖项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1060">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1061">使用 64 位 (x64) .NET Core SDK 发布 64 位应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1061">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1062">主机系统必须具有 64 位运行时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1062">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1063">ASP.NET Core 随附有 [Kestrel 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)，后者是默认的跨平台 HTTP 服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1063">ASP.NET Core ships with [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), a default, cross-platform HTTP server.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1064">使用 [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) 或 [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) 时，应用在独立于 IIS 工作进程（进程外）和 [Kestrel 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel)的进程中运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1064">When using [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) or [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), the app runs in a process separate from the IIS worker process ( *out-of-process* ) with the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1065">由于 ASP.NET Core 应用在独立于 IIS 工作进程的进程中运行，因此该模块会处理进程管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1065">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1066">该模块在第一个请求到达时启动 ASP.NET Core 应用的进程，并在应用关闭或崩溃时重新启动该应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1066">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1067">这基本上与在 [Windows 进程激活服务 (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was) 托管的进程内运行的应用中出现的行为相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1067">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1068">下图说明了 IIS、ASP.NET Core 模块和进程外托管的应用之间的关系：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1068">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![ASP.NET Core 模块](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1070">请求从 Web 到达内核模式 HTTP.sys 驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1070">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1071">驱动程序将请求路由到网站的配置端口上的 IIS，通常为 80 (HTTP) 或 443 (HTTPS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1071">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1072">该模块将该请求转发到应用的随机端口（非端口 80/443）上的 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1072">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1073">该模块在启动时通过环境变量指定端口，[IIS 集成中间件](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components)将服务器配置为侦听 `http://localhost:{port}`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1073">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the [IIS Integration Middleware](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{port}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1074">执行其他检查，拒绝不是来自该模块的请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1074">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1075">该模块不支持 HTTPS 转发，因此即使请求由 IIS 通过 HTTPS 接收，它们还是通过 HTTP 转发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1075">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1076">Kestrel 从模块获取请求后，请求会被推送到 ASP.NET Core 中间件管道中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1076">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1077">中间件管道处理该请求并将其作为 `HttpContext` 实例传递给应用的逻辑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1077">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1078">IIS 集成添加的中间件会将方案、远程 IP 和 pathbase 更新到帐户以将请求转发到 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1078">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1079">应用的响应传递回 IIS，IIS 将响应推送回发起请求的 HTTP 客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1079">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1080">`CreateDefaultBuilder` 将 [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) 服务器配置为 Web 服务器，并通过配置 [ASP.NET Core 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)的基础路径和端口来启用 IIS 集成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1080">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configures [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server as the web server and enables IIS Integration by configuring the base path and port for the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1081">ASP.NET Core 模块生成分配给后端进程的动态端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1081">The ASP.NET Core Module generates a dynamic port to assign to the backend process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1082">`CreateDefaultBuilder` 调用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A> 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1082">`CreateDefaultBuilder` calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1083">`UseIISIntegration` 配置在 localhost IP 地址 (`127.0.0.1`) 中的动态端口上侦听的 Kestrel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1083">`UseIISIntegration` configures Kestrel to listen on the dynamic port at the localhost IP address (`127.0.0.1`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1084">如果动态端口为 1234，则 Kestrel 在 `127.0.0.1:1234` 中侦听。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1084">If the dynamic port is 1234, Kestrel listens at `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1085">此配置将替换以下 API 提供的其他 URL 配置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1085">This configuration replaces other URL configurations provided by:</span></span>

* `UseUrls`
* [<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1086">Kestrel 的侦听 API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1086">Kestrel's Listen API</span></span>](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel#endpoint-configuration)
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1087">[配置](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index)（或 [命令行 -- URL 选项](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration)）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1087">[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (or [command-line --urls option](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1088">使用模块时，不需要调用 `UseUrls` 或 Kestrel 的 `Listen` API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1088">Calls to `UseUrls` or Kestrel's `Listen` API aren't required when using the module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1089">如果调用 `UseUrls` 或 `Listen`，则 Kestrel 仅会侦听在没有 IIS 的情况下运行应用时指定的端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1089">If `UseUrls` or `Listen` is called, Kestrel listens on the port specified only when running the app without IIS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1090">有关 ASP.NET Core 模块配置指南，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1090">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1091">有关托管的详细信息，请参阅[在 ASP.NET Core 中托管](xref:fundamentals/index#host)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1091">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1092">应用程序配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1092">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1093">启用 IISIntegration 组件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1093">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1094">在 `CreateWebHostBuilder` 中生成主机 ( *Program.cs* )，请调用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> 以启用 IIS 集成：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1094">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` ( *Program.cs* ), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1095">有关 `CreateDefaultBuilder` 的详细信息，请参阅 <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1095">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1096">IIS 选项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1096">IIS options</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1097">选项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1097">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1098">默认</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1098">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1099">设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1099">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1100">若为 `true`，IIS 服务器将设置经过 [Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)进行身份验证的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1100">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1101">若为 `false`，服务器仅提供 `HttpContext.User` 的标识并在 `AuthenticationScheme` 显式请求时响应质询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1101">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1102">必须在 IIS 中启用 Windows 身份验证使 `AutomaticAuthentication` 得以运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1102">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1103">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1103">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1104">设置在登录页上向用户显示的显示名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1104">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1105">要配置 IIS 选项，请在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*> 中包括 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> 的服务配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1105">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1106">下面的示例阻止应用填充 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1106">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1107">选项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1107">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1108">默认</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1108">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1109">设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1109">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1110">若为 `true`，[IIS 集成中间件](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)将设置经过 [Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)进行身份验证的 `HttpContext.User`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1110">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1111">若为 `false`，中间件仅提供 `HttpContext.User` 的标识并在 `AuthenticationScheme` 显式请求时响应质询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1111">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1112">必须在 IIS 中启用 Windows 身份验证使 `AutomaticAuthentication` 得以运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1112">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1113">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1113">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1114">设置在登录页上向用户显示的显示名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1114">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1115">若为 `true`，且存在 `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` 请求头，则填充 `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1115">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1116">代理服务器和负载均衡器方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1116">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1117">配置转发头中间件的 [IIS 集成中间件](#enable-the-iisintegration-components)和 ASP.NET Core 模块将配置为转发方案 (HTTP/HTTPS) 和发出请求的远程 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1117">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1118">对于托管在其他代理服务器和负载均衡器后方的应用，可能需要附加配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1118">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1119">有关详细信息，请参阅[配置 ASP.NET Core 以使用代理服务器和负载均衡器](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1119">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1120">web.config 文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1120">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1121">web.config 文件配置 [ASP.NET Core 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1121">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1122">发布项目时，MSBuild 目标 (`_TransformWebConfig`) 负责创建、转换和发布 web.config 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1122">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1123">此目标位于 Web SDK 目标 (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`) 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1123">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1124">SDK 设置在项目文件的顶部：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1124">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1125">如果项目中不存在 web.config 文件，则会使用正确的 processPath 和参数创建该文件，以便配置 ASP.NET Core 模块，并将该文件移动到[已发布的输出](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure)  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1125">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1126">如果项目中存在 web.config 文件，则会使用正确的 processPath 和参数转换该文件，以便配置 ASP.NET Core 模块，并将该文件移动到已发布的输出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1126">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1127">转换不会修改文件中的 IIS 配置设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1127">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1128">web.config 文件可能会提供其他 IIS 配置设置，以控制活动的 IIS 模块。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1128">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1129">有关能够处理 ASP.NET Core 应用请求的 IIS 模块的信息，请参阅 [IIS 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules)主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1129">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1130">要防止 Web SDK 转换 web.config 文件，请使用项目文件中的 \<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled> 属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1130">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1131">在禁用 Web SDK 转换文件时，开发人员应手动设置 processPath 和参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1131">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1132">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1132">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1133">web.config 文件位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1133">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1134">为了正确设置 [ASP.NET Core 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)，web.config 文件必须位于已部署应用的[内容根](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root)路径（通常为应用基路径）中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1134">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1135">该位置与向 IIS 提供的网站物理路径相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1135">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1136">若要使用 Web 部署发布多个应用，应用的根路径中需要包含 web.config 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1136">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1137">敏感文件存在于应用的物理路径中，如 \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json、\<assembly>.xml（XML 文档注释）和 \<assembly>.deps.json  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1137">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json* , *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json* .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1138">如果存在 web.config 文件且站点正常启动，则请求获取这些敏感文件时，IIS 不会提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1138">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1139">如果缺少 web.config 文件、命名不正确，或无法配置站点以正常启动，IIS 可能会公开提供敏感文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1139">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1140">部署中必须始终存在 web.config 文件且正确命名，并可以配置站点以正常启动。 **请勿从生产部署中删除 web.config 文件。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1140">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1141">转换 web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1141">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1142">如果需要在发布时转换 web.config（例如，基于配置、配置文件或环境设置环境变量），请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1142">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1143">IIS 配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1143">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1144">**Windows Server 操作系统**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1144">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1145">启用 Web 服务器 (IIS) 服务器角色并建立角色服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1145">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1146">通过“管理”菜单或“服务器管理器”中的链接使用“添加角色和功能”向导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1146">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1147">在“服务器角色”步骤中，选中“Web 服务器(IIS)”框 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1147">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)** .</span></span>

   ![在选择服务器角色步骤中选择了“Web 服务器 IIS”角色。](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1149">在“功能”步骤后，为 Web 服务器 (IIS) 加载“角色服务”步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1149">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1150">选择所需 IIS 角色服务，或接受提供的默认角色服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1150">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![在选择角色服务步骤中选择了默认角色服务。](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1152">**Windows 身份验证（可选）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1152">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1153">若要启用 Windows 身份验证，请依次展开以下节点：“Web 服务器” > “安全”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1153">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1154">选择“Windows 身份验证”功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1154">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1155">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows 身份验证 \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) 和[配置 Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1155">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1156">**Websocket（可选）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1156">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1157">Websocket 支持 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1157">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1158">若要启用 WebSocket，请依次展开以下节点：“Web 服务器” > “应用开发”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1158">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1159">选择“WebSocket 协议”功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1159">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1160">有关详细信息，请参阅 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1160">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1161">继续执行“确认”步骤，安装 Web 服务器角色和服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1161">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1162">安装 Web 服务器 (IIS) 角色后无需重启服务器/IIS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1162">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1163">**Windows 桌面操作系统**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1163">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1164">启用“IIS 管理控制台”和“万维网服务”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1164">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1165">导航到“控制面板”>“程序”>“程序和功能”>“打开或关闭 Windows 功能”（位于屏幕左侧）   。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1165">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1166">打开“Internet Information Services”节点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1166">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1167">打开“Web 管理工具”节点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1167">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1168">选中“IIS 管理控制台”框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1168">Check the box for **IIS Management Console** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1169">选中“万维网服务”框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1169">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1170">接受“万维网服务”的默认功能，或自定义 IIS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1170">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1171">**Windows 身份验证（可选）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1171">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1172">若要启用 Windows 身份验证，请依次展开以下节点：“万维网服务” > “安全”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1172">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1173">选择“Windows 身份验证”功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1173">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1174">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows 身份验证 \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) 和[配置 Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1174">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1175">**Websocket（可选）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1175">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1176">Websocket 支持 ASP.NET Core 1.1 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1176">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1177">若要启用 WebSocket，请依次展开以下节点：“万维网服务” > “应用开发功能”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1177">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1178">选择“WebSocket 协议”功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1178">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1179">有关详细信息，请参阅 [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1179">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1180">如果 IIS 安装需要重新启动，则重新启动系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1180">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

![在“Windows 功能”中选择了“IIS 管理控制台”和“万维网服务”。](index/_static/windows-features-win10.png)

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1182">安装 .NET Core 托管捆绑包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1182">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1183">在托管系统上安装 .NET Core 托管捆绑包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1183">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1184">捆绑包可安装 .NET Core 运行时、.NET Core 库和 [ASP.NET Core 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1184">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1185">该模块允许 ASP.NET Core 应用在 IIS 后面运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1185">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1186">如果在 IIS 之前安装了托管捆绑包，则必须修复捆绑包安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1186">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1187">在安装 IIS 后再次运行托管捆绑包安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1187">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1188">如果在安装 64 位 (x64) 版本的 .NET Core 之后安装了 Hosting Bundle，则可能看上去缺少 SDK（[未检测到 .NET Core SDK](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1188">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1189">要解决此问题，请参阅 <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1189">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1190">下载</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1190">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1191">导航到 [ .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) 页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1191">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1192">选择所需的 .NET Core 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1192">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1193">在“运行应用 - 运行时”列中，查找所需的 .NET Core 运行时版本的那一行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1193">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1194">使用“托管捆绑包”链接下载安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1194">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1195">某些安装程序包含已到达其生命周期结束 (EOL) 且不再受 Microsoft 支持的发行版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1195">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1196">有关详细信息，请参阅[支持策略](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1196">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1197">安装托管捆绑包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1197">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1198">在服务器上运行安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1198">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1199">通过管理员命令行界面运行安装程序时，以下参数可用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1199">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1200">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`：跳过安装 ASP.NET Core 模块。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1200">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1201">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`：跳过安装 .NET Core 运行时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1201">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1202">当服务器仅承载[独立部署 (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) 时使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1202">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1203">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`：跳过安装 ASP.NET 共享框架（ASP.NET 运行时）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1203">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1204">当服务器仅承载[独立部署 (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) 时使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1204">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1205">`OPT_NO_X86=1`：跳过安装 x86 运行时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1205">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1206">确定不会托管 32 位应用时，请使用此参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1206">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1207">如果有可能会同时托管 32 位和 64 位应用，请勿使用此参数，并安装两个运行时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1207">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1208">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`：当共享配置 (applicationHost.config) 与 IIS 安装位于同一台计算机上时，禁止对使用的是否是 IIS 共享配置进行检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1208">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration ( *applicationHost.config* ) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1209">仅适用于 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本托管捆绑程序安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1209">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1210">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1210">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1211">重新启动系统，或在命令行界面中执行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1211">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1212">重启 IIS 会选取安装程序对系统 PATH（环境变量）所作的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1212">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1213">安装托管捆绑包时，无需在 IIS 中手动停止各个站点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1213">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1214">IIS 重新启动后，托管应用（IIS 站点）也将重新启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1214">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1215">应用收到第一个请求（包括来自[应用程序初始化模块](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout)）后，将再次启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1215">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1216">ASP.NET Core 采用共享框架包的修补程序版本的前滚行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1216">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1217">当 IIS 托管的应用重新启动 IIS 时，应用会在收到第一个请求后使用其引用的包的最新修补程序版本进行加载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1217">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1218">如果未重新启动 IIS，应用会在其工作进程被回收并收到第一个请求后重新启动并显示前滚行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1218">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1219">有关 IIS 共享配置的信息，请参阅[使用 IIS 共享配置的 ASP.NET Core 模块](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1219">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1220">使用 Visual Studio 进行发布时安装 Web 部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1220">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1221">使用 [Web 部署](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later)将应用部署到服务器时，请在服务器上安装最新版本的 Web 部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1221">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1222">要安装 Web 部署，请使用 [Web 平台安装程序 (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) 或直接从 [Microsoft 下载中心](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717)获取安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1222">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1223">建议使用 WebPI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1223">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1224">WebPI 为托管提供程序提供独立的安装程序和配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1224">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1225">创建 IIS 站点</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1225">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1226">在托管系统上，创建一个文件夹以包含应用已发布的文件夹和文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1226">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1227">在接下来的步骤中，文件夹路径作为应用程序的物理路径提供给 IIS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1227">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1228">有关应用程序部署文件夹和文件布局的详细信息，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1228">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1229">在 IIS 管理器中，打开“连接”面板中的服务器节点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1229">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1230">右键单击“站点”文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1230">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1231">选择上下文菜单中的“添加网站”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1231">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1232">提供网站名称，并将物理路径设置为应用的部署文件夹 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1232">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1233">提供“绑定”配置，并通过选择“确定”创建网站：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1233">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK** :</span></span>

   ![在“添加网站”步骤中提供网站名称、物理路径和主机名。](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1235">不应使用顶级通配符绑定（`http://*:80/` 和 `http://+:80`）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1235">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1236">顶级通配符绑定可能会为应用带来安全漏洞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1236">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1237">此行为同时适用于强通配符和弱通配符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1237">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1238">使用显式主机名而不是通配符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1238">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1239">如果可控制整个父域（区别于易受攻击的 `*.com`），则子域通配符绑定（例如，`*.mysub.com`）不具有此安全风险。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1239">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1240">有关详细信息，请参阅 [rfc7230 第 5.4 条](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1240">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1241">在服务器节点下，选择“应用程序池”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1241">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1242">右键单击站点的应用池，然后从上下文菜单中选择“基本设置”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1242">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1243">在“编辑应用程序池”窗口中，将“.NET CLR 版本”设置为“无托管代码”：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1243">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** :</span></span>

   ![将“.NET CLR 版本”设置为“无托管代码”。](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1245">ASP.NET Core 在单独的进程中运行，并管理运行时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1245">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1246">ASP.NET Core 不依赖桌面 CLR (.NET CLR) 加载：将启动 .NET Core 的 Core 公共语言运行时 (CoreCLR) ，在工作进程中托管应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1246">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1247">将“.NET CLR 版本”设置为“无托管代码”是可选步骤，但建议采用此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1247">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1248">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更高版本* ：对于使用 [进程内托管模型](#in-process-hosting-model)的 64 位 (x64) [独立部署](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd)，为 32 位 (x86) 进程禁用应用池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1248">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later* : For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1249">在 IIS 管理器 >“应用程序池”的“操作”侧栏中，选择“设置应用程序池默认设置”或“高级设置”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1249">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools** , select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1250">找到“启用 32 位应用程序”并将值设置为 `False`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1250">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1251">此设置不会影响针对[进程外托管](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model)部署的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1251">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1252">确认进程模型标识拥有适当的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1252">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1253">如果将应用池的默认标识（“进程模型” > “Identity”）从 ApplicationPoolIdentity 更改为另一标识，请确保新标识拥有对应用文件夹、数据库和其他所需资源的必需访问权限  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1253">If the default identity of the app pool ( **Process Model** > **Identity** ) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1254">例如，应用池需要对文件夹的读取和写入权限，以便应用在其中读取和写入文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1254">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1255">**Windows 身份验证配置（可选）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1255">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1256">有关详细信息，请参阅[配置 Windows 身份验证](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1256">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1257">部署应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1257">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1258">将应用程序部署到 IIS 物理路径文件夹中，该文件夹是在[创建 IIS 站点](#create-the-iis-site)部分中创建的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1258">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1259">[Web 部署](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy)是建议使用的部署机制，但有几个选项可以将应用程序从项目的发布文件夹移动到托管系统的部署文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1259">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1260">在 Visual Studio 内使用 Web 部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1260">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1261">要了解如何创建用于 Web 部署的发布配置文件，请参阅[用于 ASP.NET Core 应用部署的 Visual Studio 发布配置文件](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1261">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1262">如果托管提供程序提供了发布配置文件或支持创建发布配置文件，请下载配置文件并使用 Visual Studio 的“发布”对话框将其导入：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1262">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![“发布”对话框页](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1264">在 Visual Studio 之外使用 Web 部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1264">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1265">也可以在 Visual Studio 之外从命令行使用 [Web 部署](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1265">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1266">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool)（Web 部署工具）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1266">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1267">Web 部署的替代方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1267">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1268">有多种方法可将应用移动到托管系统，例如手动复制、[Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy)、[Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) 或 [PowerShell](/powershell/)，可使用其中任何一种方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1268">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1269">有关将 ASP.NET Core 部署到 IIS 的详细信息，请参阅[面向 IIS 管理员的部署资源](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1269">For more information on ASP.NET Core deployment to IIS, see the [Deployment resources for IIS administrators](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators) section.</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1270">浏览网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1270">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1271">将应用部署到托管系统后，向应用的一个公共终结点发出请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1271">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1272">在以下示例中，站点被绑定到端口 `80` 上 `www.mysite.com` 的 IIS 主机名中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1272">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1273">向 `http://www.mysite.com` 发出请求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1273">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>

![Microsoft Edge 浏览器已加载 IIS 启动页。](index/_static/browsewebsite.png)

## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1275">锁定的部署文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1275">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1276">如果应用正在运行，部署文件夹中的文件会被锁定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1276">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1277">在部署期间，无法覆盖已锁定的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1277">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1278">若要在部署中解除已锁定的文件，请使用以下方法之一停止应用池：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1278">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1279">使用 Web 部署并在项目文件中引用 `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1279">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1280">系统会在 Web 应用目录的根目录中放置一个 app_offline.htm 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1280">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1281">该文件存在时，ASP.NET Core 模块会在部署过程中正常关闭该应用并提供 app_offline.htm 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1281">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1282">有关详细信息，请参阅 [ASP.NET Core 模块配置参考](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1282">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1283">在服务器上的 IIS 管理器中手动停止应用池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1283">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1284">使用 PowerShell 删除 app_offline.html（需要使用 PowerShell 5 或更高版本）：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1284">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```
