## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1285">数据保护</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1285">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1286">[ASP.NET Core 数据保护堆栈](xref:security/data-protection/introduction)由多个 ASP.NET Core [中间件](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)使用，包括用于身份验证的中间件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1286">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1287">即使用户代码不调用数据保护 API，也应该使用部署脚本或在用户代码中配置数据保护，以创建持久的加密[密钥存储](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1287">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1288">如果不配置数据保护，则密钥存储在内存中。重启应用时，密钥会被丢弃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1288">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1289">如果密钥环存储于内存中，则在应用重启时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1289">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1290">所有基于 cookie 的身份验证令牌都无效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1290">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1291">用户需要在下一次请求时再次登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1291">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1292">无法再解密使用密钥环保护的任何数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1292">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1293">这可能包括 [CSRF 令牌](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration)和 [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookie](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1293">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1294">若要在 IIS 下配置数据保护以持久化密钥环，请使用以下方法之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1294">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1295">**创建数据保护注册表项**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1295">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1296">ASP.NET Core 应用使用的数据保护密钥存储在应用外部的注册表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1296">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1297">要持久保存给定应用的密钥，需为应用池创建注册表项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1297">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1298">对于独立的非 Web 场 IIS 安装，可以对用于 ASP.NET Core 应用的每个应用池使用[数据保护 Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell 脚本](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1298">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1299">此脚本在 HKLM 注册表中创建注册表项，仅应用程序的应用池工作进程帐户可对其进行访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1299">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1300">通过计算机范围的密钥使用 DPAPI 对密钥静态加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1300">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1301">在 web 场方案中，可以将应用配置为使用 UNC 路径存储其数据保护密钥环。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1301">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1302">默认情况下，数据保护密钥未加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1302">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1303">确保网络共享的文件权限仅限于应用在其下运行的 Windows 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1303">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1304">可使用 X509 证书来保护静态密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1304">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1305">考虑允许用户上传证书的机制：将证书置于用户信任的证书存储中，并确保这些证书对所有运行用户应用的计算机都可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1305">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1306">有关详细信息，请参阅[配置 ASP.NET Core 数据保护](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1306">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1307">**配置 IIS 应用程序池以加载用户配置文件**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1307">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1308">此设置位于应用池“高级设置”下的“进程模型”部分 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1308">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1309">将“加载用户配置文件”设置为 `True`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1309">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1310">如果设置为 `True`，会将密钥存储在用户配置文件目录中，并使用 DPAPI 和特定于用户帐户的密钥进行保护。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1310">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1311">密钥保存在 %LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys 文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1311">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1312">同时还必须启用应用池的 [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1312">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1313">`setProfileEnvironment` 的默认值为 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1313">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1314">在某些情况下（例如，Windows 操作系统），将 `setProfileEnvironment` 设置为 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1314">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1315">如果密钥未按预期存储在用户配置文件目录中，请执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1315">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1316">导航到 %windir%/system32/inetsrv/config 文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1316">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1317">打开 applicationHost.config 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1317">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1318">查找 `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` 元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1318">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1319">确认 `setProfileEnvironment` 属性不存在，这会将值默认设置为 `true`，或者将属性的值显式设置为 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1319">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1320">**将文件系统用作密钥环存储**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1320">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1321">调整应用代码，[将文件系统用作密钥环存储](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1321">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1322">使用 X509 证书保护密钥环，并确保该证书是受信任的证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1322">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1323">如果它是自签名证书，则将该证书放置于受信任的根存储中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1323">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1324">当在 Web 场中使用 IIS 时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1324">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1325">使用所有计算机都可以访问的文件共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1325">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1326">将 X509 证书部署到每台计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1326">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1327">[通过代码配置数据保护](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1327">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1328">**设置用于数据保护的计算机范围的策略**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1328">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1329">数据保护系统对以下操作提供有限支持：为使用数据保护 API 的所有应用设置默认[计算机范围的策略](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1329">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1330">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1330">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1331">虚拟目录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1331">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1332">ASP.NET Core 应用不支持 [IIS 虚拟目录](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1332">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1333">可将应用托管为[子应用程序](#sub-applications)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1333">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1334">子应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1334">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1335">可将 ASP.NET Core 应用托管为 [IIS 子应用程序（子应用）](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1335">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1336">子应用的路径成为根应用 URL 的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1336">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1337">子应用不应将 ASP.NET Core 模块作为处理程序包含在其中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1337">A sub-app shouldn't include the ASP.NET Core Module as a handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1338">如果在子应用的 web.config 文件中将该模块添加为处理程序，则在尝试浏览子应用时会收到“500.19 内部服务器错误”，即引用错误的配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1338">If the module is added as a handler in a sub-app's *web.config* file, a *500.19 Internal Server Error* referencing the faulty config file is received when attempting to browse the sub-app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1339">以下示例显示 ASP.NET Core 子应用的已发布 web.config 文件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1339">The following example shows a published *web.config* file for an ASP.NET Core sub-app:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1340">在 ASP.NET Core 应用下托管非 ASP.NET Core 子应用时，需在子应用的 web.config 文件中显式删除继承的处理程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1340">When hosting a non-ASP.NET Core sub-app underneath an ASP.NET Core app, explicitly remove the inherited handler in the sub-app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <handlers>
      <remove name="aspNetCore" />
    </handlers>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1341">子应用内的静态资产链接应使用波形符-斜杠 (`~/`) 符号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1341">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1342">波形符-斜杠符号触发[标记帮助器](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)，来将子应用的基路径追加到呈现的相关链接前面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1342">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1343">对于 `/subapp_path` 处的子应用，使用 `src="~/image.png"` 链接的图像将呈现为 `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1343">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1344">根应用的静态文件中间件不处理静态文件请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1344">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1345">此请求由子应用的静态文件中间件处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1345">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1346">若将静态资产的 `src` 属性设置为绝对路径（如 `src="/image.png"`），则呈现的链接不包含子应用的基路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1346">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1347">根应用的静态文件中间件试图从根应用的 [web 根目录](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root)提供资产，这会导致“404 - 找不到”响应生成，除非可以从根应用获得静态资产。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1347">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1348">若要将 ASP.NET Core 应用作为子应用托管在其他 ASP.NET Core 应用下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1348">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1349">为此子应用创建应用池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1349">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1350">将“.NET CLR 版本”设置为“无托管代码”，因为将启动 .NET Core 的核心公共语言运行时 (CoreCLR) ，将应用托管在工作进程中，而非桌面 CLR (.NET CLR) 中 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1350">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1351">在 IIS 管理器中添加根网站，并且此子应用在根网站的某个文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1351">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1352">在 IIS 管理器中右击此子应用文件夹，并选择“转换为应用程序”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1352">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1353">在“添加应用程序”对话框中，使用“应用程序池”的“选择”按钮来分配为子应用创建的应用池。  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1353">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1354">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1354">Select **OK** .</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1355">使用进程内托管模型时，需要向子应用分配单独的应用池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1355">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1356">有关进程内托管模型及 ASP.NET Core 模块配置的详细信息，请参阅 <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1356">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1357">使用 web.config 配置 IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1357">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1358">IIS 配置受用于 IIS 方案（适用于包含 ASP.NET Core 模块的 ASP.NET Core 应用）的 web.config 的 `<system.webServer>` 部分影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1358">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1359">例如，IIS 配置适用于动态压缩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1359">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1360">如果在服务器一级将 IIS 配置为使用动态压缩，可通过应用的 web.config 文件中的 `<urlCompression>` 元素，对 ASP.NET Core 应用禁用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1360">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1361">有关详细信息，请参阅下列主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1361">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1362">\<system.webServer> 的配置参考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1362">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1363">要为在独立应用池中运行的各应用设置环境变量（IIS 10.0 或更高版本中支持此操作），请参阅 IIS 参考文档中[环境变量 \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) 主题下的“AppCmd.exe 命令”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1363">To set environment variables for individual apps running in isolated app pools (supported for IIS 10.0 or later), see the *AppCmd.exe command* section of the [Environment Variables \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) topic in the IIS reference documentation.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-sections-of-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1364">web.config 的配置节</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1364">Configuration sections of web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1365">ASP.NET Core 应用不会使用 web.config 中的 ASP.NET 4.x 应用的配置部分进行配置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1365">Configuration sections of ASP.NET 4.x apps in *web.config* aren't used by ASP.NET Core apps for configuration:</span></span>

* `<system.web>`
* `<appSettings>`
* `<connectionStrings>`
* `<location>`

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1366">会使用其他的配置提供程序配置 ASP.NET Core 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1366">ASP.NET Core apps are configured using other configuration providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1367">有关详细信息，请参阅[配置](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1367">For more information, see [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span></span>

## <a name="application-pools"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1368">应用程序池</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1368">Application Pools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1369">在服务器上托管多个网站时，建议在每个应用自己的应用池中运行各应用，以彼此隔离。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1369">When hosting multiple websites on a server, we recommend isolating the apps from each other by running each app in its own app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1370">IIS“添加网站”对话框默认执行此配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1370">The IIS **Add Website** dialog defaults to this configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1371">提供了站点名称时，该文本会自动传输到“应用程序池”文本框 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1371">When a **Site name** is provided, the text is automatically transferred to the **Application pool** textbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1372">添加站点时，会使用该站点名称创建新的应用池。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1372">A new app pool is created using the site name when the site is added.</span></span>

## <a name="application-pool-no-locidentity"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1373">应用程序池 Identity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1373">Application Pool Identity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1374">通过应用池标识帐户，可以在唯一帐户下运行应用，而无需创建和管理域或本地帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1374">An app pool identity account allows an app to run under a unique account without having to create and manage domains or local accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1375">在 IIS 8.0 或更高版本上，IIS 管理员工作进程 (WAS) 将使用新应用池的名称创建一个虚拟帐户，并默认在此帐户下运行应用池的工作进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1375">On IIS 8.0 or later, the IIS Admin Worker Process (WAS) creates a virtual account with the name of the new app pool and runs the app pool's worker processes under this account by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1376">在 IIS 管理控制台中，确保应用池“高级设置”下的“Identity”设置为使用 ApplicationPoolIdentity  ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1376">In the IIS Management Console under **Advanced Settings** for the app pool, ensure that the **Identity** is set to use **ApplicationPoolIdentity** :</span></span>

![应用程序池“高级设置”对话框](index/_static/apppool-identity.png)

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1378">IIS 管理进程使用 Windows 安全系统中应用池的名称创建安全标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1378">The IIS management process creates a secure identifier with the name of the app pool in the Windows Security System.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1379">可使用此标识保护资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1379">Resources can be secured using this identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1380">但是，此标识不是真实的用户帐户，不会在 Windows 用户管理控制台中显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1380">However, this identity isn't a real user account and doesn't show up in the Windows User Management Console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1381">如果 IIS 工作进程需要对应用的高级访问权限，请为包含该应用的目录修改访问控制列表 (ACL)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1381">If the IIS worker process requires elevated access to the app, modify the Access Control List (ACL) for the directory containing the app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1382">打开 Windows 资源管理器并导航到目录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1382">Open Windows Explorer and navigate to the directory.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1383">右键单击该目录，然后选择“属性”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1383">Right-click on the directory and select **Properties** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1384">在“安全”选项卡下，选择“编辑”按钮，然后单击“添加”按钮  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1384">Under the **Security** tab, select the **Edit** button and then the **Add** button.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1385">选择“位置”按钮，并确保该系统处于选中状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1385">Select the **Locations** button and make sure the system is selected.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1386">在“输入要选择的对象名称”区域中输入 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1386">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1387">选择“检查名称”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1387">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1388">有关 DefaultAppPool，请检查使用 IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool 的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1388">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1389">当选择“检查名称”按钮时，对象名称区域中会显示 DefaultAppPool 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1389">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1390">无法直接在对象名称区域中输入应用池名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1390">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1391">检查对象名称时，请使用 **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** 格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1391">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![应用文件夹的“选择用户或组”对话框：在选择“检查名称”前，将“DefaultAppPool\"”的应用池名称追加到对象名称区域中的“IIS AppPool”。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1393">选择“确定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1393">Select **OK** .</span></span>

   ![应用文件夹的“选择用户或组”对话框：在你选择“检查名称”后，对象名称“DefaultAppPool”显示在对象名称区域中。](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1395">默认情况下应授予读取 &amp; 执行权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1395">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1396">根据需要请提供其他权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1396">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1397">也可使用 ICACLS 工具在命令提示符处授予访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1397">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1398">以 DefaultAppPool 为例，使用以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1398">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1399">有关详细信息，请参阅 [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) 主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1399">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1400">HTTP/2 支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1400">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1401">满足以下基本要求的进程外部署支持 [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1401">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported for out-of-process deployments that meet the following base requirements:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1402">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 或更高版本；IIS 10 或更高版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1402">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1403">面向公众的边缘服务器连接使用 HTTP/2，但与 [Kestrel 服务器](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel)的反向代理连接使用 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1403">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1404">目标框架：不适用于进程外部署，因为 HTTP/2 连接完全由 IIS 处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1404">Target framework: Not applicable to out-of-process deployments, since the HTTP/2 connection is handled entirely by IIS.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1405">TLS 1.2 或更高版本的连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1405">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1406">如果已建立 HTTP/2 连接，[HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) 会报告 `HTTP/1.1`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1406">If an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1407">默认情况下将启用 HTTP/2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1407">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1408">如果未建立 HTTP/2 连接，连接会回退到 HTTP/1.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1408">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1409">有关使用 IIS 部署的 HTTP/2 配置的详细信息，请参阅 [IIS 上的 HTTP/2](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1409">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1410">CORS 预检请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1410">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1411">本部分仅适用于面向 .NET Framework 的 ASP.NET Core 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1411">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1412">对于面向 .NET Framework 的 ASP.NET Core 应用程序，默认情况下，IIS 不会将 OPTIONS 请求传递给应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1412">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a6d40-1413">若要了解如何在 web.config 中配置应用程序的 IIS 处理程序以传递 OPTIONS 请求，请参阅[在 ASP.NET Web API 2 中启用跨域请求：CORS 的工作原理](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a6d40-1413">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>
